One strong point of this class is that the positive affective aspects are apparent in the checklist. By
creating a supportive classroom environment, she tries to lower students' affective filter and reduce
anxiety. One weak point, on the other hand, is shown the second criteria in the instructional strategies
that the teacher uses. She uses an inappropriate grouping strategy for group activities.
Consequently, the lower-level students would feel difficulties when they perform the task even though
higher-level ones follow the stages without any problems.
In view of the instructional strategies what the teacher uses, the lower-lever students have difficulty in
completing  the  task  with  unclear  directions  and  inappropriate  activities  for  them.  To  solve  these
problems, the teacher should provide the students with clear directions on what they are required to
do on task. For example, she could give linguistic ques or show more detail guidance on processing
the task. Second, the level-appropriate activities are required for the lower-level learners. Task allows
students to concentrate on how they achieve things they already learned thus, too difficult tasks are
not helpful to acquire the proper function of the task.

problems. Second, the current news style is different from great literature and theater in that the latter
employs strong characters to make audience think about larger moral and social situations in critical
terms  whereas  the  former  rarely  makes  people  engage  in  serious  social  issues  because  of  its
systematic tendency to personalize social, economic, and political situations.

Requirement  2  :  The  deverbal  suffix  -al  must  be  added  to  the  verb  base  having  a  [+anterior]
consonant(segment) as a coda of the final syllable.
Requirement 3: The deverbal suffix -al must be attached to the verb base ending in a [+anterior] sound
preceded by a I-sonorant] sound.
The structured input activity in <B> is based on the Lexical Preference Principle.
In this activity, students are exposed to the pairs of sentences in the activity, in which each pair has
the same lexical meaning but different tenses. Thus, it requires them to focus on the lexical meaning
first  and  the  form  (the  past  tense  marker  -ed)  second.  In  other  words,  through  a  form-meaning
relationship in this activity, they distinguish the present from the past tense by noticing the past tense
marker "-ed, resulting in naturally processing it.
Figure 2 represents the fluctuations in sheep population, which shows stable status over a hundred
years. The lesser fluctuations of the population of sheep are due to their larger size and longer lifespan
(which make them less affected by changes in environment and birth rate respectively.)
The theme of the poem is maintaining morale and hope despite many difficulties and hardship in the
course of achieving a goal. To illustrate the theme, the speaker employs a central metaphor of 'the
main,  which  represents  the  great  goal(success)  achieved  by  overcoming  all  the  difficulties  and
adversity. (The speaker conjures the image of "the main," which is the sea raising up with the tide after
being fed by “creeks and inlets." While the waves appear to crash again and again in the same spot,
there is a greater force feeding and steadily raising it)
It is inevitable that Korea becomes an aging society. Koreans are required to
prepare in order to effectively deal with their longer life expectancies. In terms of the individual level,
people in Korean should embrace healthier lifestyles for the following two reasons. First off, healthy
living not only improves one into old age but also improves the outlook and effectivity of the individual
through their whole life. This means a better outlook, improved mental health and physical ability. A
second reason to pursue health-oriented lifestyles is that keeps one away from unhealthy excesses or
vices. Bad habits such as smoking or excesses drinking are detrimental to the individual
To meet the needs of a larger elder population Korea should develop its pension system.
First, by creating an expanded safety net for senior citizens, we would see alleviation on the pressures
placed onto younger generations to support their parents and grandparents. This will have a positive
effect  on  the  whole.  Secondly,  an  expanded  pension  system  would  mean  retirees  can  leave  the
workforce and give employment the young. while caring for the elderly. In these two ways an expanded
relief system can address this tough issue of Korean aging well.

The  underlined  parts  in  (2)  and  (3)  are  regarded  as  constituents  when  we  consider  the  tests  of
substitution and movement. As for (2), both substitution and movement are applied: the underlined
part is replaced with the pronoun ‘them’ (or ‘those’) and it undergoes rightward movement because
of its heaviness (because it is a heavy NP). In (3), though the underlined part may not be moved as
in ‘.. *crowded with ___ from Asia ..’, it can be substituted with the pronoun ‘those’.
 이  문제는  지시  사항이  다소  혼란스러운데,  movement  and/or  substitution 이라는  말은  결국  답인

이건  매우  어려운  문제임. (아마  대부분 4 점  만점에 2 점대나  그  이하에  머물렀을  수도)

Requirement 3 가  어려운데  이와  관련해서는  오래  전에 Siegel (1979: 164-168)에서  이런  경우  접어

첨가  조건을  아래와  같이  정식화  했음에  주목하면  일단  핵심은  다  들어간  것임.

강세  모음 + (공명음인  자음) + 순치음, 치음, 치경음  중  한  개

괄호는 optional

Requirement 3 에서  윗  줄은  이  조건을  다  준수한  데이터들이라  적형이  되고

아랫  줄은  이  조건을  어김, 특히  중간에  비공명음인  자음이  옴

그리고  이런  것들  역시 Requirement 2 에서와  마찬가지로 Anterior 속성  연결해서  설명됨

채점  기준: Requirement  2 에서  적형이  되는  곳  이유  설명 (1 점)  +  R2 에서  비적형이  되는  곳  이유

6

설명 (1 점) + R3 에서  적형이  되는  곳  이유  설명 (1 점) + R3 에서  비적형이  되는  곳  이유  설명 (1 점)
The teaching procedure in <B> focuses on The Lexical Preference Principle in that it deals with the
problem of focusing on only meaning while ignoring the linguistic form, the past tense marker ‘-ed’ in
this case. The structural input activity in <B> contributes to students’ correct processing of the target
form for meaning in that it provides them with the opportunity to notice the target form ‘-ed’ while they
are checking whether each example sentence includes a present or past verb form.

채점  기준: <B>의  교수  절차가  집중하는  원칙이  어휘  선호  원칙임을  찾아냄 (0.5 점)  + 이  원칙이

해당되는  데  대한  적절한  이유를  서술 (1 점)  +  <B>에서의  구조화된  입력  활동이  학생들이  대상

1

형태를  적확하게  인식하는데  도움되는  근거를  적절히  서술 (1.5 점)
Figure B demonstrates the fluctuation of sheep population in terms of its
stability,  period,  and  number  agreement  with  the  text.(주제문에도  이런  구체적  서술  있어야  점수

of 100 years and the minimum 1,230.000 and the maximum 2.250.000. The sheep population was so
stable because sheep have great home pager iis and undergo little change due to environment. The
fluctuation of their short-time birth rate contributes little to the overall population because they live
long.

#  비교적  안정적인  등락폭을  보여야  하고

(한  가지만  적절히  설명하면  1점)

#  항상성이  뛰어나고  환경에  의한  생리적  변화가  적다

#  수명이  길어서  출산율이  단기적  변화가  숫자에  영향  별로  안  준다

2

This  poem  asserts  that  we  should  not  complain  about  difficulties  with  pessimism  in  the  course  of
achieving a great goal. but that we should struggle for the goal.
In the former two stanzas, the narrator reproaches the negative thoughts of abandoning the struggle
against hardship while he encourages us to have hope in the great goal in the latter two stanzas. The
metaphoric expression, "the main" contributes to reinforcing this theme in that it represents the great
goal achieved through overcoming hard challenges. The main". therefore. is the rationale for us
to endure and overcome all the difficulties.
3점:  주어진  시의  요지를  본문의  근거를  제시하며  적절하게  설명했다.

요지  자체만  서술하거나  본문의  근거가  되는  내용  일부만  나열하면  1.6점  서술을  시도했으나

대체로  미흡하면  0.6점

#  이  시의  요지:  어려움  혹은  힘든  목표와  맞서  싸우면서  부정적으로  생각하지  말고

끝까지  분투하면  반드시  성취/성공할  수  있다.

#  본문에서  근거:  첫  두  연에서는  힘든  목표를  이룰  수  없다고  부정적으로  말하지  말  것을

요구하고  있음.  후반부  두  연에서는  끝까지  참고  싸워나가면  위대한  성취가  다가올  것을  말하고

있음.

2점:  지적된  the main이  갖는  은유적  의미를  시의  요지와  관련해서  적절하게  설명했다.

아래  설명을  다소  불충분하게  설명하면  1점  서술을  시도했으나  대체로  미흡하면  0.6점

We  should  develop  life-long  hobbies  such  as  playing  musical  instruments,  performing  dances,  or

hiking,  against  the  old  age  (단락  전체  주제  문장도  이렇게  구체적으로!!  안  그러면  당연히  감

점)First, these hobbies can improve out health in body and soul when we continues those until old

ages. They provide us with refreshment in mind and proper functions in body. Second, these hobbies
can be good leisure time activities when we have few works to do in old age. Most senior citizens have
no or few works to fill their leisure time, which makes their lives most untolerable. The hobbies above

can  be  efficient  tools  to  fill  the  boring  time.(여기서  보듯  각  근거도  주제  문장이  두괄식으로  앞서

제시되고  그  뒤에  뒷받침  문장  1-2개  정도  배치,  이런  요소들  다  있어야함.  다음  단락에서도  마

찬가지임.)As for the societal level. we should re-examine mandatory retirement age in financial and

affective dimensions. First, in this aging society we should be able to have more time to earn money
for the remaining life. When forced to live without income for such a long retirement life, our lives will
be  extremely  hard.  Second,  we  should  consider  the  self-esteem  that  may  be  lewered  because  of
earlier retirement. When we cease to work any longer, we tend to feel ourselves useless in the society.

To minimize the sense of deprivation. we should postpone the time of retirement. (둘째  단락에서도

전체  주제문이  구체성을  지녔는지.  각  근거별로  소주제문과  뒷받침  문장은  안  빠지고  서술했는

지  점검.  이  모든  게  점수임.)그리고  이  문제는  고령화  사회에  대해  해박한  지식은  아니라도  상

The strong point of this class is the use of interesting materials as checked "3" in the list. This is proved
especially by the note about the fun video clip. That is described as "SS loved it". The weak point, on
the other hand, is found in terms of same ability grouping, which is checked as "I' in the list. Though
higher-level students had no problem, the lower-level ones had difficulty in task completion, with no or
little  help.  as  cited  in  Notes.  To  address  the  problem  of  the  lower-level  group,  task  grading  and
scaffolding by the teacher are required. (<=  여기서도  주제  문장을  막연하게  '두  가지  대책이  필요

하다  라는  식으로만  쓰면  당연히  감점) First, grading or adjusting the facility (difficulty) of the task is

required for efficient language acquisition. (<=  첫  대안의  주제문도  이  정도는  구체적으로  써야함!)

Too difficult (or to simple) tasks are not helpful for students to acquire the target function. We should
adjust the task facility so that students can understand the target function without too much learning
load. Second, the teacher should provide students with proper scaffolding to overcome the difficulties,
through linguistic cues for speaking in English or more obvious guides about the task. With such help,
students can achieve the success in the task and enhance their language

I firmly believe that developing life-long hobbies can keep old people vigor in terms of psychological
aspect. First of all, old people can be vigorous by getting involved in life-long hobbies. The reason
why old people feel boring is because they do not have anything to immerse. They can be alive by
doing hobbies. Secondly, old people can maintain their relationship through life-long hobbies. The
biggest problem with old people is that they feel isolated. They have a sense of frustration and
loneliness. By climbing mountains or going fishing, they can keep in touch with their old friends.

From the perspective of the societal level, we should reform the healthcare system. The biggest
reason is that being cured when people are sick is one of the basic rights that all human beings
should be guarantted. The reason why people pay taxes is that the government offers public
services. Another reason is that compared to two other options in the question, it costs less money
and does not results in any conflicts between young generations and old generations since young
generations are eager to get a job nowadays.
The strong point of Kim Sumi's teaching is that she makes a warm atmosphere. By showing
multimedia materials which students loved, lower people can easily comprehend the contents. Also,
teacher's kind personality can lower the students' anxiety. By lowering their anxiety, students can
easily ask questions and answer the questions. The weak point is that she put the same level of the
students in the same group, so that lower level students cannot complete the task.
The problems that the lower level students have are that they cannot comprehend the task and
complete the task. In order to solve these problems, the teacher can mix the different students into a
same group, so that high level students can provide scaffolding to lower level students. In addition,
the teacher can adapt the task for lower level students with easier words and visual aids.

위의  답안은  채점되지  않았습니다.  또한  2014  답안이  모든  카페에  하나밖에  없어서  이거라도  올립니다.
